# SpiderMonkey JIT Compilation Pipeline

## Your Task

A new contributor wants to understand how Firefox's SpiderMonkey JavaScript engine compiles JS to optimized native code. Find all key C++ source files in `mozilla-firefox/firefox` that define the JIT compilation pipeline stages: 1. The file that implements the top-level `IonCompile` function which orchestrates the Ion optimizing compiler (in `js/src/jit/`). 2. The header and source files for `IonCompileTask` — the off-thread compilation task (in `js/src/jit/`). 3. The file that defines `BaselineJIT` — the first-tier JIT compiler (look for `BaselineScript` class in `js/src/jit/`). 4. The header that defines `JitRuntime` — the per-runtime JIT state (in `js/src/jit/`). 5. The file that defines `JitOptions` — JIT configuration (in `js/src/jit/`). Report the repo, file path, and key class or function name for each file.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the onboarding domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've successfully identified all the key C++ source files in Firefox's SpiderMonkey JavaScript engine that define the JIT compilation pipeline stages. Here's a summary of the findings:

## Key JIT Compilation Pipeline Components:

1. **IonCompile function** (`js/src/jit/Ion.cpp:1765`)
   - Top-level orchestrator of the Ion optimizing compiler
   - Initializes MIRGraph, CompileInfo, and MIRGenerator
   - Delegates to `StartOffThreadIonCompile` for background compilation

2. **IonCompileTask class** (`js/src/jit/IonCompileTask.h` and `IonCompileTask.cpp`)
   - Off-thread compilation task representing a single Ion compilation
   - Inherits from `HelperThreadTask` and `mozilla::LinkedListElement<IonCompileTask>`
   - Contains MIRGenerator reference, CodeGenerator pointer, and WarpSnapshot

3. **BaselineScript class** (`js/src/jit/BaselineJIT.h:189`)
   - First-tier JIT compiler representation
   - Stores baseline-compiled method code and warm-up check offsets
   - Maintains reference to pending `IonCompileTask` for lazy linking

4. **JitRuntime class** (`js/src/jit/JitRuntime.h:121`)
   - Per-runtime JIT state manager
   - Maintains `ionLazyLinkList_` for pending Ion compilation tasks
   - Manages trampoline code, exception handlers, and JIT infrastructure

5. **JitOptions configuration** (`js/src/jit/JitOptions.h` and `JitOptions.cpp`)
   - `DefaultJitOptions` struct defines all JIT configuration flags
   - Global `JitOptions` instance controls runtime compilation behavior
   - Includes settings for Baseline, Ion, OSR, inlining, and optimizations

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with comprehensive file paths, symbol names, and a detailed narrative explanation of how these components work together in the JIT compilation pipeline.
